 krishna ko mewa, maakhan or misari behad priy hai

 ) If your hair is long and thick, then you will be well aware that washing hair in the rain is not less of a problem
 ek ore jahaan is mausam main bal jaldi sookhte nahin hai vahiin der tak geele pade baalo se badboo bhi aane lagati he
 The smell coming from the hair is very strong
 darasal, ye badboo nami kii vajah se hi hoti he
 After washing the hair, when they remain wet for a long time, they start to smell
 agar baalo kii nami der tak bani rahati he to isse fungal infections hone kaa khatra bhi bad jaataa he
 Fungal infections cause hair roots to weaken and hair fall begins
 aise main koshish karen ki baalo main nami rukne na paae
 Dry the hair as soon as possible after washing it
 badboodaar baalo kii pareshaani dur karne ke liye apanaaen ye upaay:1
 Clean the scalp thoroughly while washing hair
 infections se bachane ke liye anti-fungal yaa anti-bacterial shampoo yuj karen
 If you want, you can also use water from basil leaves
 2
 Use things containing vitamin c in your diet

 3
 agar aap bahut adhik chaay yaa coffee leti hai to uskaa intech kam kar den
 Consuming too much of a cold drink or a soft drink can be dangerous
 4
 Do not let hair stay wet for too long
